	<h1 class="entry-title">Tier List Maker | Tier maker without watermark | Create your own tier list</h1></header><!-- .entry-header -->

<div class="entry-content single-content">
	
<p></p>


<div id="BlankRectlify"></div>



<p>Have You tried using any online tier list makers and became frustrated because of the exhausting login walls just to find out that the tier list that you&#8217;ve been working on since a few hours has a logo when you try to save it? I have, and let me tell you, I don&#8217;t like it. A Tier List Maker should be simple, easy to use, No Pay or login walls and provide an option to save the tier list as an image!</p>



<p>This prompted me to create this tool which allows you to do just that with no extra work. This tool is designed to be user friendly and has all the features that the other tier makers have. But without any bloatware like login to create a tier or any logo on the tier list. Above is the tier list maker, Enjoy!!!</p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column85_ebe437-a2"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="kt-adv-heading85_38f693-71 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading85_38f693-71">How to Use Tier List Maker</h2>
</div></div>



<p></p>



<p>Watch the following Explainer Video </p>



<figure class="wp-block-embed is-type-video is-provider-youtube wp-block-embed-youtube wp-embed-aspect-16-9 wp-has-aspect-ratio"><div class="wp-block-embed__wrapper">
<iframe title="🚀 Create EPIC Tier Lists in MINUTES | NO Watermark | Tier List Maker - The Ultimate Tool for Ranking" width="720" height="405" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/nIxQNlvpJZQ?feature=oembed" frameborder="0" allow="accelerometer; autoplay; clipboard-write; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture; web-share" referrerpolicy="strict-origin-when-cross-origin" allowfullscreen></iframe>
</div></figure>



<h5 class="kt-adv-heading85_81f638-c0 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading85_81f638-c0">Creating a tier list with free Tier List Maker is simple and straightforward. Follow these steps to get started:</h5>



<ul class="wp-block-list">
<li><strong>Create from a Blank Template:</strong> Just click on the upload images button to upload your images from your computer or copy paste images from the web/Computer.</li>



<li><strong>Choose a Template:</strong> Select a template from below or search it using search button above.</li>



<li><strong>Customize Tiers:</strong> Adjust the text of tiers, rename them, and change their colors.</li>



<li><strong>Add or Remove Tiers:</strong> Right click and then Press Delete Tier to delete a tier similarly click the + button to add Tiers.</li>



<li><strong>Drag and Drop:</strong> Arrange your Images into the appropriate tiers using your mouse or finger (Long Press on an image with your finger).</li>



<li><strong>Save as an Image:</strong> Save your tier list to your computer with save as image button and share with the world.</li>



<li><strong>Enjoy your Custom Tier list with watermark!</strong></li>
</ul>

<h5 class="kt-adv-heading85_a6aab2-0f wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading85_a6aab2-0f">Tier List Maker offers a plethora of features to enhance your tier list creation experience:</h5>



<h3 class="kt-adv-heading85_9724d2-7d wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading85_9724d2-7d">Create Unlimited Tier Lists</h3>



<h5 class="kt-adv-heading85_502a1a-fb wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading85_502a1a-fb">With Tier List generator, there are no limits to your creativity. You can create as many tier lists as you want on any subject. Whether it&#8217;s a one-time ranking or a series of lists, Tier List Maker has you covered.</h5>



<h3 class="kt-adv-heading85_b01e20-d6 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading85_b01e20-d6">Community Templates</h3>



<h5 class="kt-adv-heading85_bae532-ca wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading85_bae532-ca">Explore a vast collection of templates created by our team members. These templates cover a wide range of topics, from gaming and entertainment to sports and lifestyle. You can use these templates as a starting point for your tier lists or get inspiration for new ones.</h5>



<h5 class="kt-adv-heading85_1f2887-bc wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading85_1f2887-bc"></h5>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column85_cc6a87-19"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="kt-adv-heading85_129837-14 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading85_129837-14">FAQs</h2>
</div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-accordion alignnone"><div class="kt-accordion-wrap kt-accordion-id85_5280da-54 kt-accordion-has-9-panes kt-active-pane-0 kt-accordion-block kt-pane-header-alignment-left kt-accodion-icon-style-basic kt-accodion-icon-side-right" style="max-width:none"><div class="kt-accordion-inner-wrap" data-allow-multiple-open="false" data-start-open="none">
<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-1 kt-pane85_b36fd5-6f"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title">What is a Tier List maker online?</span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>A tier list is a method of ranking items, characters, or concepts based on their relative quality, performance, or preference. Tiers are usually labeled from highest to lowest (e.g., S, A, B, C, D) to categorize the items being ranked.</p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-2 kt-pane85_8e4f02-ad"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title">Is Tier List Maker free to use?</span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>Yes, Tier List Maker is completely free to use. You can create, customize, and share your tier lists without any cost.</p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-3 kt-pane85_124820-6d"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title">Can I collaborate with others on a tier list?</span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>Not now but we plan on adding collaboration features soon.</p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-4 kt-pane85_90ef21-ab"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title">How do I share my tier list?</span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>Once you’ve created your tier list, you can export it as an image and share it on social media, forums, or any other platform of your choice.</p>
</div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-pane kt-accordion-pane kt-accordion-pane-5 kt-pane85_b6874b-c8"><div class="kt-accordion-header-wrap"><button class="kt-blocks-accordion-header kt-acccordion-button-label-show" type="button"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title-wrap"><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-title">Can I save my tier lists?</span></span><span class="kt-blocks-accordion-icon-trigger"></span></button></div><div class="kt-accordion-panel kt-accordion-panel-hidden"><div class="kt-accordion-panel-inner">
<p>Yes, you can save your tier lists to your account and revisit them anytime. This allows you to update or revise your rankings as needed.</p>
</div></div></div>
</div></div></div>



<p></p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column85_f0b696-1a"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="kt-adv-heading85_ac1e04-b9 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading85_ac1e04-b9">Conclusion</h2>
</div></div>



<h5 class="kt-adv-heading85_40fb67-ee wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading85_40fb67-ee">Tier List Maker is the perfect tool for anyone looking to create detailed and visually appealing tier lists. With its user-friendly interface, extensive customization options, and ability to export and share lists, it is the ideal platform for expressing your rankings on any topic. Join the Tier List Maker community today and start creating your ultimate tier lists!</h5>
